			"T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T",
			"G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","A","C","T","A","T","G","T","A","T","A","T","G","C","A","T",
			"A","T","G","T","A","C","A","T","A","T","G","T","G","T","A","T","G","T","T","C","A","T","A","T","A","T","A",
			"C","A","T","A","C","A","T","A","C","A","T","A","T","A","T","A","C","A","A","T","G","A","A","C","T","A","C",
			"A","A","C","C","C","C","A","A","C","C","C","C","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C",
			"C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T",
			"A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C",
			"C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C",
			"T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A",
			"C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C",
			"T","A","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T",
			"A","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","G","A","G","A","C","T","G","T","A","T","T","T","T","G","G","T",
			"A","C","C","C","T","T","T","G","G","G","T","A","A","A","T","A","C","C","T","A","A","T","A","G","T","G","A",
			"C","A","T","T","G","C","A","T","G","C","A","C","C","C","A","A","T","A","T","T","T","A","C","A","G","C","A",
			"G","C","A","T","T","A","T","C","A","A","C","A","G","T","A","G","C","C","A","A","A","C","T","A","T","G","G",
			"A","G","A","A","A","G","C","C","C","A","A","G","T","A","T","C","C","A","T","C","A","A","C","T","G","A","T",
			"G","A","A","G","G","T","G","T","A","A","A","G","A","A","G","T","T","G","T","G","G","G","G","T","G","T","G",
			"T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T",
			"G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","A","C","T","A","T","G","T","A","T","A","T","G","C","A","T",
			"A","T","G","T","A","C","A","T","A","T","G","T","G","T","A","T","G","T","T","C","A","T","A","T","A","T","A",
			"C","A","T","A","C","A","T","A","C","A","T","A","T","A","T","A","C","A","A","T","G","A","A","C","T","A","C",
			"A","A","C","C","C","C","A","A","C","C","C","C","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C",
			"C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T",
			"A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C",
			"C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C",
			"T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A",
			"C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C",
			"T","A","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","C","T",
			"A","A","A","C","C","C","T","A","A","C","C","G","A","G","A","C","T","G","T","A","T","T","T","T","G","G","T",
			"A","C","C","C","T","T","T","G","G","G","T","A","A","A","T","A","C","C","T","A","A","T","A","G","T","G","A",
			"C","A","T","T","G","C","A","T","G","C","A","C","C","C","A","A","T","A","T","T","T","A","C","A","G","C","A",
			"G","C","A","T","T","A","T","C","A","A","C","A","G","T","A","G","C","C","A","A","A","C","T","A","T","G","G",
			"A","G","A","A","A","G","C","C","C","A","A","G","T","A","T","C","C","A","T","C","A","A","C","T","G","A","T",
			"G","A","A","G","G","T","G","T","A","A","A","G","A","A","G","T","T","G","T","G","G","G","G","T","G","T","G",
			"T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T",
			"G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","G","T","A","C","T","A","T","G","T","A","T","A","T","G","C","A","T",
			];
	

			for(var i = 0; i < _sizeView; i++){
				dataset.push(_baseData[i + _viewIndex]);
			}
							
			//Create SVG element
			var svg = d3.select("body")
						.append("svg")
						.attr("width", _w)
						.attr("height", _h);


			svg.selectAll("rect")
				.data(dataset)
				.enter()
				.append("rect")
			    .attr("x", function(d, i) {
					
					return i * (_w / dataset.length);
				})
				.attr("y", 0)
				.attr("width", _w / dataset.length - _barPadding)
				.attr("height", 100)
				.attr("fill", function(d) {
					var color ="";
					switch(d){
						case "A":
						color = "rgb(0, 200, 0)";
						break				
					case "T":
						color = "rgb(200, 0, 0)";
						break
					case "G":
						color = "rgb(255, 255, 0)";
						break
					case "C":
						color = "rgb(0, 0, 200)";
						break
					default:
						color = "rgb(0, 0, 0)";
						break
					}
					return color;
				});				

				
			if((_w / dataset.length) > 10 ){
				svg.selectAll("text")
					.data(dataset)
					.enter()
					.append("text")
					.text(function(d) {
						return d;
					})
					.attr("text-anchor", "middle")
					.attr("x", function(d, i) {
						return i * (_w / dataset.length) + (_w / dataset.length - _barPadding) / 2;
					})
					.attr("y", 14)
					.attr("font-family", "sans-serif")
					.attr("font-size", "11px")
					.attr("fill", function(d) {
						if (d == "G"){
							return("black")
						}
						else
						{
							return("white")
						}
				   });
			}
			
			function scrollToLeft(stepSize){
					_deleteFromTail(stepSize);
					_addToHead(stepSize);
					_reRenderingView();	
				};
			function scrollToRight(stepSize){
					_deleteFromHead(stepSize);
					_addToTail(stepSize);
					_reRenderingView();						
						
				};
			function zoomPlus() {
					var size = Math.ceil(dataset.length / 4);
					_deleteFromTail(size);
					_deleteFromHead(size);					
					_reRenderingView();	
				};
			function zoomMinus() {
					var size = Math.ceil(dataset.length / 2);
					_addToTail(size);
					_addToHead(size);					
					_reRenderingView();	
				};
				
			function _reRenderingView(){
				
				
				var bars = svg.selectAll("rect")	//Select all bars	
					.data(dataset);	
					
				bars.enter()								//References the enter selection (a subset of the update selection)
					.append("rect")							//Creates a new rect					
					.attr("y", 0)
					.attr("height", 100)
					.attr("x", _w)
					.attr("width", _w / dataset.length - _barPadding)
					.attr("fill", function(d) {
						var color ="";
						switch(d){
							case "A":
							color = "rgb(0, 200, 0)";
							break				
						case "T":
							color = "rgb(200, 0, 0)";
							break
						case "G":
							color = "rgb(255, 255, 0)";
							break
						case "C":
							color = "rgb(0, 0, 200)";
							break
						default:
							color = "rgb(0, 0, 0)";
							break
						}
						return color;
				});
				//Update
				bars.transition()							//Initiate a transition on all elements in the update selection (all rects)
					.duration(500)
					.attr("y", 0)
					.attr("height", 100)
					.attr("x", function(d, i) {
						return i * (_w / dataset.length);
					})
					.attr("width",  _w / dataset.length - _barPadding)
					.attr("fill", function(d) {
						var color ="";
						switch(d){
							case "A":
							color = "rgb(0, 200, 0)";
							break				
						case "T":
							color = "rgb(200, 0, 0)";
							break
						case "G":
							color = "rgb(255, 255, 0)";
							break
						case "C":
							color = "rgb(0, 0, 200)";
							break
						default:
							color = "rgb(0, 0, 0)";
							break
						}
						return color;
					});
					//Exit
				bars.exit()				//References the exit selection (a subset of the update selection)
					.transition()		//Initiates a transition on the one element we're deleting
					.duration(500)
					.attr("x", function(d, i) {
						return -i * (_w / dataset.length);
					})	//Move past the right edge of the SVG
					.remove();   		//Deletes this element from the DOM once transition is complete
					

				if((_w / dataset.length) > 10 ){	
				
					var labels = svg.selectAll("text")
						.data(dataset);
						
					labels.enter()
						.append("text")
						.text(function(d) {
							return d;
						})
						.attr("text-anchor", "middle")
						.attr("x", _w)
						.attr("y", 14)					
						.attr("font-family", "sans-serif")
						.attr("font-size", "11px")
						.attr("fill", function(d) {
						if (d == "G"){
							return("black")
						}
						else
						{
							return("white")
						}
						});	

					labels.transition()
						.duration(500)
						.text(function(d) {
							return d;
						})
						.attr("x", function(d, i) {
							return i * (_w / dataset.length) + (_w / dataset.length - _barPadding) / 2;
						})
						.attr("fill", function(d) {
						if (d == "G"){
							return("black")
						}
						else
						{
							return("white")
						}
				   });						
					//Exit	
					labels.exit()
						.transition()
						.duration(500)
						.attr("x", -(_w / dataset.length))
						.remove();					
				}	
				else
				{
					var labels = svg.selectAll("text")
						.data(dataset);
						
					labels.enter()
						.append("text")
						.text("")
						.attr("text-anchor", "middle")
						.attr("x", _w)
						.attr("y", 14)					
						.attr("font-family", "sans-serif")
						.attr("font-size", "11px")
						.attr("fill", function(d) {
						if (d == "G"){
							return("black")
						}
						else
						{
							return("white")
						}
						});	

					labels.transition()
						.duration(500)
						.text("")
						.attr("x", function(d, i) {
							return i * (_w / dataset.length) + (_w / dataset.length - _barPadding) / 2;
						})
						.attr("fill", function(d) {
						if (d == "G"){
							return("black")
						}
						else
						{
							return("white")
						}
				   });						
					//Exit	
					labels.exit()
						.transition()
						.duration(500)
						.attr("x", -(_w / dataset.length))
						.remove();
				}				
			};
			
			//TODO
			function _deleteFromHead(stepSize){
				dataset.splice(0, stepSize);  //Delete from view non-visibility nucleotides
				_viewIndex += stepSize;
				_increaseView(stepSize)
			}
			//TODO
			function _addToTail(stepSize){  			
				_decreaseView(stepSize)
				debugger;
				for(var i = _viewIndex + dataset.length; i < _viewIndex + _sizeView; i++){ //Add to view new visibility nucleotides
					dataset.push(_baseData[i]);
				}
			}
			//TODO
			function _deleteFromTail(stepSize){
				dataset.splice(dataset.length - stepSize, stepSize);  //Delete from view non-visibility nucleotides
				_increaseView(stepSize)
			}
			//TODO
			function _addToHead(stepSize){  
			debugger;
				_viewIndex -= stepSize;
				_decreaseView(stepSize)
				for(var i = _viewIndex; i < _viewIndex + stepSize; i++){ //Add to view new visibility nucleotides
					dataset.unshift(_baseData[i]);
				}
			}
			function _increaseView(stepSize){
				_sizeView -= stepSize;
				if(_sizeView < _maxSizeForPadding){
					_barPadding = 1;
				}
			}
			function _decreaseView(stepSize){
				_sizeView += stepSize;
				if(_sizeView > _maxSizeForPadding){
					_barPadding = 0;
				}
			}
			
			
			
		</script>
	</body>
</html>
